dou retenement de l’urine	holding back urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or similar conditions that we have discussed in the previous section. If the urine is not released and you see the obstruction caused by the stone located at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent forward at the waist, with his feet placed on his back, his stomach pressed down from above the waist, and the patient straining as hard as he can. This will force the neck of the bladder upward, causing the stone to be expelled, and the urine to flow; if this does not happen as described, and the patient experiences great pain, then you should use a device called a "syringe", made as follows: it should have a thin, flexible silver shaft, like the feather of a bird; the tube should be about a palm and a half in length, with a thin tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way to remove the urinary obstruction is to take a double thread and tie at the end a piece of wool or cotton, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe; and squeeze out the excess wool and insert it into the syringe up to the tip, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk; then have the patient sit on a seat, and apply the oil moistened with olive oil and warm water to the bladder and penis; then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the abdomen; then fill the syringe all the way up to the bladder, and feel the patient's bladder being emptied into the syringe; if this is not done in this order, the person guiding where the syringe goes is doing it wrong; then tie off the thread at the wool, and the urine will follow the wool; then remove the syringe, and let the urine flow out; and reinsert the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When there are cuts or bleeding in the bladder, or when pus is accumulated, and you see the fluids and medications dripping, then do all the instruments that are called "clepsydra", and this is how it is formed:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see. The location where the medicine enters should be such that it blocks the penis well without addition, so that moisture can be extracted and re-inserted when needed; and when you see your medicines flowing into the bladder, put the tip of the syringe into the moisture, and draw it out while pushing it in; thus, you will extract the moisture with the syringe and then push it strongly back in. The moisture will now enter and come to the bladder, so that the patient can feel it. This is the form of the subtle enema by which one enemas the bladder. Thus:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or brass, and its head is higher; below, there is one testicle or two; then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture in it that you want to use to enema the bladder, then tie it between the two testicles with a thin double string, and heat this moisture over the fire; then insert the tip of the enema into the penis, and squeeze your hand on the bladder gently, so that all the moisture comes in until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder. If you don't have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make it into a circle, and pierce it all around; then insert the string tightly through these openings, then assemble the circle as one assembles a wheel, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument. Do as you did with the bladder, squeezing your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division of stones, and their extraction together with medicines; and I have described the difference between a stone lodged in the ureter, and all the signs, and in which kind of stone one should operate with cutting; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will now tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the urine flows from the bladder like water in its subtlety; and it causes pain in the penis, and the patient may urinate many times, and then the flow stops; and many of these have the hernia; and the cure is much easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the feces that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes blocks the search for stones.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him around so that the stone descends into the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from above; then let him sit between your hands which are prepared, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downward; then probe and touch inside; if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut upon the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with the touch, then wet your index finger of the left hand with oil, if the patient is fat, or your middle finger, if the patient is thin and fully grown; then insert it into their anus, and probe for the stone, and when you feel it at your finger, push it up to the neck of the bladder; then press against your finger, and move it out where you intend to cut.Et li doins de la main drete soit sus le col de la vessie por l’esguarder que la piere ne descende en la vessie.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And command the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and command the patient to extend his testicles upward with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin beneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum, of which this is the shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they make an incision between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the scrotum; and let it be straight on the stone, and both testicles should be pressed against the anus, and let the incision be diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, according to the size of the stone, not too large; by chance the pressure on the testicle which is against the anus may cause it to burst without any effort; and know that there is a kind of stone which has angles and edges: it is difficult to remove. And there is another kind which is round like a pebble, and its extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	Therefore, when you have one with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not burst, then you must grip it with tongs which are like a file at the tip, to extract the stone so that it does not escape; or you insert under the instrument a thin, curved hook; and if you cannot grasp it in this way, then enlarge the opening of the urethra, and if the blood comes out, stop it with vitriole; and if there is more than one stone, then insert first the largest into the neck of the bladder, then push the rest upward, and then draw them out.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be sewn, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Because there are two things that can happen to the patient: they may die, or their urine may flow out from where the skin cannot heal; but nevertheless, try to pull it, or scrape it away with tweezers, as much as you can; and when you have finished your work, apply incense, aloe, and dragon's blood to the wound, and constrict it, and place a moistened cloth in oil and wine, or oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then resew the wound on their neck, and do not untie the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you remove it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with ointment of diaphenicon and basilicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions of blood come to the wound and congealing of blood in the bladder, and it is retained by this means in such a way that urine passes with the urine: then push your finger into the wound and draw out that blood, for if it remains there, the bladder will be corroded and burst; then wash the wound with water and vinegar, and aid the patient in every way you know how until he is healed; and it is fitting that every hour that you treat him, you tie his two thighs together and assemble remedies over the wound.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and it is in the urethra, stuck in place, and the urine cannot pass through; then the treatment of what I am saying is that you cut it many times with a knife, and this cutting by this treatment is an excuse for not cutting it.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have experienced this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take a piece of iron according to this form, and let it be pointed at three angles, and fix it into a stick:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and wind it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot return to the bladder; then push the awl into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone; then turn the awl in your hand inside the stone a little at a time, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then the urine will come out soon, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is still inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once, and comes out with the urine, then the patient is healed; but if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a string under the stone and another above it, then stretch the penis over the stone between these two strings, then pull it out, and untie the string, and cleanse the frozen blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	Sometimes stones become stuck in women, and if they do, the cure is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who can be examined by midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman well skilled in this art of midwifery; and the fourth way is that the woman's stone is more deeply embedded than a man's, so it requires a deeper incision, and great fear is involved. And if necessity arises, one should take a midwife who is well skilled, and with difficulty extract the stone from her, and if you cannot extract it, do not want to use a very fine probe; and present a wise woman knowledgeable about midwifery or a woman skilled in part of the art, and instruct her to do what you direct according to your examination of the stone; and be sure to check whether the woman is a virgin. Then she should press her finger into the vagina and seek out the stone; and if she finds it, she should grip it beneath her finger, and I instruct her to press her left hand firmly over the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If she has a hernia, it is necessary to move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder down to the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the groin, where the muscle is most tender, and feel for the stone in that area; and do not move your finger on top of or below the stone, and let the incision be small at first. Then pour wine into the incision if you feel the stone has been cut so that it can come out, and know that there are many types of stones: some are small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and some have hairs.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	[and] know their appearances in order to identify the type [of stone].
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood does not stop flowing, then put ground vitriol on the wound and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work until the stone is removed, and have at hand the instruments I have told you about in the extraction of stones from men so that they can assist you in your task. And if the blood does not stop and it is an artery that has been cut, then put the powder on the wound and apply pressure with bandages and tourniquets; do not touch the stone again or try to pull it out, lest the patient die. Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the wound has healed, return to your work until the stone is expelled.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Aquous pus is nothing else but an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is located beneath the heart of the testicles and contains the sperm; and it is called "pus", and sometimes it is found within the membrane of the testicle, as if it were another testicle; and what we have said is the skin of the testicle between the white pus. And this does not usually happen.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the cause of this disease is from weakness which comes to the testicles, and that matter is spread about.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors: or it is jaundice-colored, or redless, or black, or watery white, and it happens more; and these are the signs of recognizing this assembly, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have said, then the abscesses are reason, a little long as the shape of an egg, and does not appear to the testicles, because it has moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the testicle itself, then the abscesses are reason with part of an egg, and because of this one thinks it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then one feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, try all the intrusions, from which the form is as mentioned before.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the foreskin, judge what is inside it.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he lies on his back on something slightly raised, and many folds of cloth are placed beneath him; then he sits up on his left side, and he commands the attendant to sit on his right, and stretches out the rod to one of the two ribs near the heart; then take the spatulum, and lift the skin of the breast among them from the long end down to the armpit, and let this incision be straight while cutting the skin of the breast up to the white of the armpit, and tear it gently according to its strength; then pierce the armpit with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and stretch the armpit upward; and do not touch the heart of the breast, but only the armpit; lift up all around it carefully, for if you do not lift it well, the water will return; and if the egg jumped out during your work, then return it to its place when you have finished the work of the armpit; then join the two lips of the breast with a single stitch, then cure it as other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the testicle corrupted by some other disease, then you must tie off the vessels that are suspended, fearing an effusion of blood; then cut the testicle away at its very suspension, and extract it, and dress the wound as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	If the wound is split into two parts, know that these are the branches; then bandage the other part as you did the first, then wash with blood, and put soft wool soaked in rose oil into the wound; and put another piece of soft wool soaked in wine and oil over it, and place the two pieces of cloth on top, and put doubled sheets on top of them, and tie it up around the entire wound according to this form.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of cloth, and stuff them with wool according to this pattern and have them sewn together at the crotch of the breeches, and one end placed under the buttock up to the back, and the other end at the groin; and the two other ends over the two angles, and tie the entire bandage around the waist of the breeches; and sometimes medicine this branch with cauterization instead of iron, and take a thin cultellaire cautery, and scorch the skin of the branches, and it will be revealed white like water; then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that white part at the joints, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And the cup in every way that you can, as long as you stretch everything out; and be careful that the fire does not touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move while guarding against blood flow, and changes in the incision of the wound; and if nothing makes you contrary, or abscesses or blood flow or anything else, then cure what makes you contrary, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment due to its horribleness, then administer the perforation as I told you, and it is when you are well assured by the signs that we have said that the water is gone, then let the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess in the part below all the spasm large, and place the perforation deep into the body; and make the holes wide so that all the water flows out; then put cotton over the area, and bandage it, and leave it to drain the remaining water, then treat the wound until it heals; and if the white film does not let the water out through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat water in the sick, of which the shape is described earlier; and widen the wound, and know that the water will return, and be gathered after six months or around there, and when it is gathered as before, and thus the patient will pass their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the incision of this branch there is fear in many dispositions, because of which it seems better to leave it; and I will tell you the work and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	So I say that many abscesses come from the body, especially in the groins; and this is due to various causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is what you need to know: it can be caused by an excessive build-up of bile or phlegm, or by a blow; and the color of the abscess depends on the color of the body; and there is no pain, and it is a serious abscess; and sometimes there are gray, fearful, and pus-filled abscesses, with a flowing color, and at times it comes from a vein, or from inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is due to a vein, it is recognized by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and you should not touch it.Quant c’est par enfleure de voine, si est conus quant li voins se rompent et fuient par l’aposteme, et les voins sont vides, et ne peut mie fuyr plus.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are made of swelling of the vein are known by their appearance and touch with both hands, and anyone can well make the incision on this appearance and on other characters; and you should cut the heart of the eggs, then the yolks are on top, and the white part is forced out from under, and the suspension is released from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the egg is already cooked with these necessary characters, then you must cut the egg and the heart; and if there is air in the white or in that which is inside the vessels, then you must release all of that membrane and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the egg's yolk is at the back, you must scoop it all out and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, apply the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then cure it with other cures until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to an onion, with the softening of the testicles, and the patient grieves greatly when he moves; and the cure for this disease is also prepared as fearfully as that one before, and nevertheless we will tell you its operation according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to have the patient sit on a raised seat, then tie the suspensory band of testicles down with your fingers, around all the vessels that are close to the penis, and constrict them tightly; then pierce with a broad, sharp spatula through the vessels, as far as they can be uncovered, and then scrape each side, just as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein appeared, and tie it directly to the other end; then pierce them straight in the middle, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then cure the wound as with the others or with a bowstring, so that no vessel is torn that nourishes one of the testicles; for through this no harm comes, and if veins come from all the vessels, then the testicles should be tied to all the vessels; so that the urethra does not lose its nourishment due to the piercing of the vessels, and dry up and cannot heal.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rutting of the syphilis
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The causes of this hernia are from the rupture that occurs in the diaphragm, or from the extension over the abdomen in the region of the intestines, causing them to descend from this opening to one of the sides; and this opening is in the diaphragm, or from its extension, and these two types of hernias occur from many causes: from a blow, or from jumping, or from coughing, or from lifting a heavy load, and similar activities. The sign that it is from an extension in the diaphragm is that it occurs slowly over a long time, and does not happen suddenly; and the hernia is equal in size up to the depth, because the diaphragm pushes down on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is of the section of the sinus that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear diverse below the skin, and this is due to the exit of the intestine and the body from the sinus.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with it, and are retained inside, and cause great suffering to the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cures of iron there is fear, from which one should escape.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the way to treat it is to instruct the patient to pull the intestine back into the wound with his hand if he can; then hold the neck between your hands and lift the buttocks; then the chest will be above, and stretch all the skin of the groin; then insert the fingers of the hand into the opening in the abdomen according to what is needed to open the wound, so that the bowel can come out; then scrape off the hernia that is under the skin of the scrotum, until the white hernia sac is exposed all over; then put your index finger into the one that is next to the testicle, between the white hernia sac which is under the skin of the egg, and between the second hernia sac, and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second hernia sac; then move with your right hand into the groin, and hold the white hernia sac in your left hand, and lift the testicle up to the hernia sac; and tell the assistant to pull the testicle up, and untie what is behind the bandage; and feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped around the hard white hernia sac, and if you find anything, put it back into the abdomen; then take a needle with a thick thread made from ten threads, and insert it into the back part of the hernia sac, which is under the skin of the scrotum; then grasp the heads of the threads, so that there are four threads; then tie them together in a cross pattern, and tie the hernia sac, which we said was under the skin of the scrotum, with two strong ties from two parts; then wrap up the thread around the groin, and tie it tightly in two places, so that none of the vessels that supply blood to it can enter, or an abscess will form there; then put the bandage back on according to the first long band, two fingers from that one; and after those two ties, leave the hernia sac under the skin of the scrotum hanging loose as before; then grasp the part under the skin of the scrotum, so that the blood runs, and the bowel, as we said earlier; then apply soft wool soaked in oil to the wound, and put on the bandage that we mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white ulcer we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this happens many times, and leaves the lien as long as it weeps through it; and if it is slow to fall off, then make an incision with a hot needle and apply what we have said until it falls out; then cure the wound with another cure until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch of medicine, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients say that it is made like a ram's horn which is joined to the vein, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the incision above, lightly from below; then cut into it, and cure the abscess with what was said, until the vessels weep; and cure it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes there is a rupture in the intestines, as we have said, and the place opens up; but none of the intestines come out, and if any do come out, it is only a little, and they need to be repaired every hour; and even if he remains too long at this point, the wound will fester, because of the extension of the syphilis which is in the intestines, as we have said, for it is extended, then softened and swollen, and the place opens up; and it is cured by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is cured with iron in this way: and you must make the patient lie on his back between your hands, then cut into the place of the rupture, filled with salt according to the amount of three fingers; then draw out the syphilis which is under the skin, then take the thread and put it over the visible place of the syphilis; and press it deep into the abdomen, then sew up the two visible places of the syphilis on the head of the thread, and sew them both; then pull out the head of the thread, and do not cut into the syphilis or extend anything, as I have made you aware in the cure for a rupture of the intestines; then cure it with the cure for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syphilis is restrained, and has no appearance in the buttock, and the cautery is more effective in this area, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of softening the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men because the parts inside become soft, and it is milky in appearance; and when one wishes to treat it, one should make the patient lie on his back, and cut the soft skin over the scrotum; then sew together the two edges of the wound with a single stitch, or two stitches or four, firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the sutures.
dou chastrement	chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is forbidden in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to mention it in this book; but it is necessary for two reasons. The first is so that physicians can answer questions about it, and know how to perform the operation; the second is because we often have need of castrating certain animals to help us, such as bucks, rams, and horses and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say therefore that castration is performed in two ways: either by twisting, or by cutting.Chastremens fait selonc l’atraction des testicules, et de la chair qui est entre li codis et li testicules; car il n’est pas necessaire que tu fasses fendre selonc li testicules ou selonc la chair, mes ains tu atractions selonc la chair.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In the method we perform by twisting, we have the animal sit in warm water until the scrotum becomes soft and dangling; then we squeeze them with our hand until they are pulled back up and we can no longer feel them.Et quant la chair soit atrainie tant qu’elle soit lieve et que li testicules soient remontiez, tu les retreins tout a ta main si fort qu’il te poit, si com tu ferois un fil d’or ou d’argent; puis retreins les testicules si fort qu’il te point, si com tu ferois li testicules.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Of the castration of a male: you should hold the animal and press the scrotum in your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cup each testicle with one hand, when you have scooped them well; and leave some pus from the syphilis and the subtle syphilis which is on the vessels; and this method of castration is gentler than that made by attraction, because with attraction something of the testicles may remain, making the animal desire lust; then cure the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in men: one is that between the two testicles there appears as the figure of a woman, with hair, and sometimes it urinates like a man; another is where a man has the appearance of a woman but with male genitalia, and in this case, he has no sperm.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other way occurs in women, where there is a penis and testicles above the vagina.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment of men and women is that you dress the wounds on their genitals, and treat them as other wounds; in the second manner, of men whose urine leaks through the skin of their scrotums, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A tentingene is a wound on the natural part, as far as it is too ugly to look at; and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You should dye the excess of the tentingene with your hand or nails, and cover it lightly; and do not go too deep, lest bleeding occur, then cure other wounds until it is healed; and for another wound that arises at the mouth of the wound, and use it, and perhaps it will fester, and is according to the appearance of a boil, and therefore the ancients called it the "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you need to treat it, as we have said, perform the ten-tige, and the treatment until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratica
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	Erratique is when the nature of a woman is not understood, or the opening is small; it can be natural from birth, or accidental due to illness where it occurs; or it could be caused by a foreign object, or an ulcer that is thin or thick, and forms a deep wound in the womb, or on the sides, or below, wherever it may be; and they should understand conception and childbirth, and sometimes flowers too; and knowledge of this comes from observing a woman's dance.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the stoppers are visible nearby, you can reach them with your fingers or a stick.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is a thin ulcer and it is close to the lips, you can treat it like this: put your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips into a tube so that the thin ulcer is exposed and covered by the stoppers; then take some wool, moisten it in oil, and place it over the area, and have the woman lie at home every day so it does not close up.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the ulcer is hard and thick, then you must cover it with a spatula like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is of new flesh, then stop it at once and cover it; and have stanching medicines like oak-galls, dragon's blood, incense, and a mixture of egg; then apply a broad piece of linen, so that the wound may not heal over; and let this be for a long time, and then apply a tent of dry linen; then cure with other cures until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is new flesh in the wound, it must be covered thus, unless it is an abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not touch an abscess that is in a wound.Si li apestemens est en la marris, si le covient coper et fere sanz touc de fer; car selonc que ce soit encheancrez, li doit on mettre un trusiau d’argent en la tete del aposteme; si sera mievant a l’aposteme.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins from which blood flows freely without a bandage, and when hemorrhoids are old they become thrombosed; and we have already described their appearances like ears, and the signs, and I will now describe those that respond to treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and thrombosed veins, when they are fully formed in the anus, and do not appear to be felt, except for the cure by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the anus, which one can feel, are those that one can cure.Quant il sont em parfont et ne sentent mie, si n’est poignante, et il ne puet curer.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	It is necessary, therefore, to place the woman in a cold room; then the hemorrhoids are pressed with tweezers and the vein cut at its roots; then powder is applied with medications that restrain bleeding, such as acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and similar things; then her feet are bathed in water for an hour, and then she is placed in cold water; and if bleeding occurs, she should sit in a decoction of sumac, pomegranate bark, gales, and similar things, and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and make a poultice to be applied to her back.Quant il sont em parfont et non entamer en l’altelul, si li convient boire la manze de saige, et aler sus le chemin, ou c’est grant tort, et li convient boire la manze de seson.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is stopped, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	If not, then have leeches applied to the back and breasts without bleeding; then take woolen cloth, soak it in juice of plantain or in juice of dogwood with old wine, and apply it to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the abscess has drained, then treat the wound with ointment until it is healed; and that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles a hard lump, so it should be covered as I have said; and then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of anal abscesses
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses arise in the body, such as ulcers and pus-filled abscesses and herpes and skin conditions and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have described in the classification.Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	It is therefore necessary that I discuss in this treatise the hot abscess which occurs in the stomach, which is not one of the abscesses that form in the bowels; and if you wish to know the treatment with fire, then observe whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, and filled with heat and fever, and whether it turns red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	Therefore, do not be in a hurry to pierce it, but let it drain until the pain is relieved; and then have the patient sit on a chair, with two small chairs to lean on, and support his back and press his feet against the ends of his legs; and let his thighs be spread out, and place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good rope; then suck the abscess towards the right side, and introduce the instrument to open the mouth of the abscess, from which the pus will come out afterwards; and it is necessary that when you introduce this instrument, you insert the rod first to feel the depth of the abscess, so that the instrument does not go in further than it should, and so that it does not hurt the patient; and if the instrument is larger, then cover the depth of the abscess with cloth so that it is not painful to the patient; and one must hold the funnel of the instrument upwards, and tighten the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.	And when the abscess is opened and it is done with a gentle hand, then it must be covered with a bandage, or with the spatulum, gently; and when the bowels are evacuated, then you must put into the wound wet dressings in rose oil, or in dry green oil; and place the dressing outside of the wound at the bottom of the wound, and place a poultice over the wound and over the wound a clean linen cloth moistened with water or malva flowers that have been cooked; then heal after two days of ointment, until it is cured; and sometimes raise the wound and the wound by enema of water and honey, and then of water or roots of lilies and aristolochia that have been cooked for a long time; then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is sunken in the wound, then you must be careful to avoid burning with hot iron, but heal it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	It is necessary for the midwife to know the appearance of a natural childbirth, and the signs that it is about to occur when you see the woman push downward and desire to smell aromatics; then hasten the baby's emergence; then you will know that this childbirth is according to nature, and the afterbirth will follow with the baby, and the mother's excess fluids will be expelled through proper cleansing; and this one who comes otherwise does not come naturally.

Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the child emerges head-first in a natural delivery, but the woman is struggling and weak, then seat her on a stool or have other women support her. And if the hands come out, then you must gently push them back in a little bit at a time; and if they cannot go in, then put the woman on a chair, and raise her feet up high; then tip the chair onto its front legs, and hold the woman so she doesn't fall over; and if the hands still cannot go in, and the child is dead, then scratch the hands with the nail that was mentioned before, and pull out the child, and then reset everything as before.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of a child upon his feet

de l’issue des gemelz	of the twin's birth

Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote; puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be pulled back due to the dislocation, then you must wrap a cloth around it, until it is healed; then apply the cupping on the palm or on the wrist, and you should do the same for the other hand, and also for the feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue; ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui; et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment; et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer; et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues; et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if the child's head is large and it is straining to come out, or if it has a sharp pain gathered in its head, then you should put the spathumile between your fingers, open up the head, and extract the fluid; or you may use the instrument called 'almidach', from which the mold comes with the instruments that follow this one. And so also do if the child has a large natural head; and then pull the bones apart with tweezers, and if the head pops out and is forced, let it split until the fluids that are in the birth canal flow out; and if it cannot come out, pierce it into pieces as much as you can; and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you should pierce it so that the fluids run out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, the pulse is light, and the healing is swift at the mouth of the wound.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main; et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre; et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris; puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer; et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses; et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And if it is straining in the belly or vagina, then you should draw it out wrapped in a cloth held by your hand; and open up the belly or vagina so that the fluids within flow out; and if other parts are stuck and the head remains inside, then insert the tip of your finger into the back of the mouth, and pull it towards the front; then insert a nail or two, and pull it out; and if there is an abscess in the back of the throat causing narrowing, then one should not work on it, but rather apply moist and greasy substances; and administer poultices, and use warm and softening fluids.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif; et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if the child is on its side, and you can bring it to an equal level, then do as we said about the living child; but if one cannot, then cut it into pieces and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris; et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And when you have done this, if the treatment for abscesses that come in childbirth is administered, and blood flow occurs, it should be stopped with a string, and other treatments should be applied.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly some children had been dead, then another was sewn onto it, and the others died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came to her in the groin, and swelled so much that it burst open, and began to emit a foul odor.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the priest, and I thought long, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a strong attracting plaster, and an bone came out, and after a few days, some more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point; et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu; et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	I wanted to investigate the wound, and I felt around inside with my hands until the woman was in a better state; she lived for a long time afterwards, and then one day she suddenly died; and I don't recall this chapter being used except that when masters encounter something strange, they know how to provide relief.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the dislocated back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here after comes the form of the press, to which one applies books; and at .2. turns for .2. chaps of .2. strings.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux; et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi; et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus; et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	Nevertheless, the horn should be more slender than the restrictor, and it should be made of boxwood or ebony; and the mouth of the tube should be two fingers wide, and its edges should be half a palm long; and in both ends there should be two adjustments of this same wood, which are fixed in one end and moveable in the other, about half a palm long or a little more; and these two adjustments are inserted into the mouth of the woman to open it when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles; et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large; et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes; puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Another form, with its appearance more subtle and lighter, is made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the appearance of tongs; and has at both ends two adjustments, as you see, a palm long, and two digits wide; and when you see open the wound all over the instrument, then let the woman lie on the bed, her feet hanging and her legs open, then fit the two adjustments together in the wound, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs; then work your hand over the instrument, as you have done with tongs similarly, according to the amount that you see open the mouth of the wound, until the woman does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all tipped and have multiplied their appearances; and when the surgeon has prepared them, the work is faster and higher in men due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair of the instrument that you have not prepared, for its necessity is inexcusable.
